###  Töyräs₁

This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Töyräs* (FIXME)
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  41
* Origin:  finer
* Possible NER class:  LAST
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
